# claude-mgr — project context for Claude Code sessions

A **read-mostly governance CLI** for the user's large Claude Code harness (inventory / conflicts / `config show-effective` / doctor / snapshot-rollback / remove-update). Zero-runtime-dependency Node ESM, Windows-hardened, **dry-run-by-default**, lives OUTSIDE Claude Code's loader. The user is a non-coder ("vibe coding") — reply in Chinese.

- **Full plan (1624 lines):** `C:\Users\alice\.claude\plans\claude-mgr-v5.md` — the single source of truth (decided-items table + verified loader rules + 67-unit schedule + test catalog).
- **Session memory / decisions / learnings:** `C:\Users\alice\.claude\projects\C--Users-alice\memory\MEMORY.md`.

"pgdown","f","d"`)→翻页而非跳转——用户自然按小写,故两个都"不跳"。**测试盲区**:`TestHKeyJumpsToHealth`/`TestDKeyNavigatesToDispositions` 发的是**大写** `"H"`/`"D"`(实现者视角),正好命中能跳的 case,从没验证小写=真实用户按键。**修复**:`case "h","H"`→健康、`case "d","D"`→处置建议(大小写都跳);从两个翻页处理器移除 `d`(翻页保留 `f`/`PgDn`);状态栏 `1-0/←→`→`1-0/H/D/←→`(截图暴露的可发现性缺口:tab 栏有 H/D 但状态栏没提)。新 `TestMnemonicsAreCaseInsensitive`(发小写 h/H/d/D 断言各自跳=能抓此 bug 的证伪 oracle,对旧码两腿全红)。SEPARATE -File "<script>.ps1"`——共享分类器 `findScriptArg` 的"第一个非选项词=脚本"通用规则会把 `-ExecutionPolicy` 的**值** `Bypass` 误当脚本 → doctor #3 假"文件缺失"ERROR。修法 = `hook-command.mjs` 加**解释器作用域**的 node/python/bash **字节不变**(`grammar &&` 全短路);共享修复两个目标皆受益。**descriptor 增 `hookSource`**(claude=`settings-merge`、codex=`json-file:hooks.json→.hooks`)→ NEW `src/cli/effective-hooks.mjs` Journal = `{journalVersion,planVersion,command,snapshotId,targetClaudeDir,state,createdAt,updatedAt,ops}`. `createJournal` (pure) redacts each op via `redactPatchOp` BEFORE storage so no plaintext secret persists — pinned by a zero-leak oracle (plaintext absent from the serialized journal) + independent sha256 golden anchors; non-sensitive op fields (e.g. create `content`) kept verbatim for replay. `TRANSITIONS` (Object.frozen): planned→{snapshotted,failed} · snapshotted→{applying,failed,rolled-back} · applying→{committed,failed,rolled-back} · committed→rolled-back · failed→rolled-back · rolled-back=terminal; **INVARIANT `planned↛rolled-back`** (a rollback restores FROM a snapshot, captured only at `snapshotted`). `transition` (pure) is IMMUTABLE — returns a NEW journal (ops shared by reference, never mutated), same-ref unchanged on an illegal move. `writeJournal` (gated I/O, REQUIRED+fail-safe injected `assertWritable` ctx `'apply'` like lock.mjs/manifest-io, verify-after-write byte-compare) + `readJournal` (ENOENT→`journal-not-found`, top-level proto-key strip, refuses FUTURE journalVersion). Never-throws throughout. code-reviewer (opus) APPROVE **0 Blocker/0 High**; adopted MEDIUM (wrap `serialize` in the write-failure path — a non-sensitive UNSERIALIZABLE op value e.g. BigInt would otherwise throw at JSON.stringify, breaking never-throws; pinned by a regression test) + 3 LOW (constructor/prototype proto-strip coverage, write-path `../escape` traversal assertion, ops-by-reference contract test). ⚠ sibling follow-up: `writeManifest` (snapshot-manifest-io.mjs:85) shares the same `serialize`-outside-try gap but its values are hashes so it is ~unreachable — guard if touched. commits `bc57b7d`/`754cdf8` pushed; **1107 tests / 0 fail** (+38), lint/invariants/boundary clean. **P3.U3 DONE** (2026-05-27 — pure logic + static data, gate-safe; first SNAPSHOT-machinery unit) — the secrets allowlist + matcher. `src/config/secrets-allowlist.json` (transparent+extensible per threat-model H2): `extensions` (crt/cer/pem/key/p12/pfx/gpg/asc) · `exactNames` (id_rsa/id_ed25519/id_ecdsa/id_dsa/credentials/.credentials.json/.env) · `globNames` (.env.* / *token.json / *secret.json / *oauth.json / *-credentials* / *-token* / *-oauth* / *-secret* — every entry MUST contain `*`). `src/lib/secrets-allowlist.mjs` — pure never-throws `matchesSecret(path,allowlist?)→{match,kind,pattern}` + `isSecretFile`; matches on BASENAME (so a sensitive ANCESTOR dir can't drop a clean nested file like `skills/api-tokens/SKILL.md`), case-insensitive, order extension→exact→glob; loads the JSON via `import … with {type:'json'}`; injectable allowlist seam. createSnapshotTar issues `tar -c` for chunk 0 then `tar -r` (append) per subsequent chunk, every chunk re-gated by safeSpawn. **UNICODE-SAFETY PIVOT the integration test FORCED**: bsdtar `-r` CORRUPTS non-ASCII member names on Windows (append reads argv via the OEM codepage: café→café-se_or) while `-c` marshals wide-chars correctly — so the chunker forces ALL non-ASCII members into chunk 0 (the only `-c` chunk) and appends ONLY ASCII via `-r`; a mismatch (the atomic-write CRASH WINDOW: target absent / content differs) REFUSES (`recover-resume-unverified`) + recommends `--rollback` — **structurally cannot false-commit** (the opsLanded gate strictly precedes the transition+write); per-op containment under targetClaudeDir before any read; 0-op vacuously verified, multi-op refused (P3.U19). **`--rollback`** (journal-AWARE): read the journal, require a legal `→rolled-back` edge (refuse `planned`=no snapshot / `rolled-back`=done / missing=recommend --from-manifest), wrap the U17 `rollbackSnapshot` (lock→drift→verify→restore), persist `rolled-back` ONLY after a successful --apply restore (a post-restore journal-write failure → ok:false, live tree already restored, state stays `applying`). **`--from-manifest`** (journal-AGNOSTIC, the DoD HEADLINE): restore from the manifest+tar ALONE (rollbackSnapshot never reads the journal — verified across all its sub-units) so a CORRUPTED/missing journal STILL recovers, then BEST-EFFORT reconcile the journal (a bad journal never fails a good restore). **DRY-RUN BY DEFAULT** (enableWrites gates the restore + journal write); the M2 crash window (target absent + journal `applying`) is handled for free (the snapshot holds the ORIGINAL bytes; the missing file reads as deletion-drift so recovery needs `--force`); stranded `.mgr-new`/`.mgr-old` sidecars are gc/doctor#21's job, not recover's. Windows backslash/UNC/drive escapes, the resume hash-gate, dry-run, journal reconciliation, no --mark-failed regression [byte-equivalent codes], result-shape consistency, falsifiable tests); 1 LOW (a malformed injected seam returning `{ok:true}` w/o `code` → made `code` consistent via `rb.code ?? (rb.ok?CODE.ok:CODE.error)`) ADOPTED, 2 LOW (gate-required-on-dry-run = documented design choice [CLI always injects]; from-manifest post-restore read = intentional best-effort, no redundancy) no-change. **DoD acceptance oracle GENUINE** — `test/integration/recover-from-manifest.test.mjs` RAN (NOT skipped) with the REAL `assertWritable` (CLAUDE_CONFIG_DIR→temp) + REAL system tar: (1) a CORRUPTED apply-journal.json + a mutated live tree → `--from-manifest --apply --force` restores CLAUDE.md+settings.json byte-identical from the manifest, reports `recover-from-manifest-no-journal` (not fatal), residue-free; (2) a journal stranded at `applying` + the target DELETED (crash window) → `--rollback --apply --force` restores the file from the snapshot's original bytes + the on-disk journal re-reads `rolled-back`. NEVER attempted, message recommends `recover --rollback`), apply does NOT auto-rollback already-written ops. The commit-incomplete case (writes LANDED but the final `committed` transition/persist failed) STAYS `applying`+`applied:true`+`ok:false` for `recover --resume` (preserved through `commitApply`). The DEFAULT (no `enableWrites`) path stays BYTE-IDENTICAL (stops at `snapshotted`). **(2) `--paranoid`**: after each successful write, if the target basename ends `.json`, re-READ from disk + `parseJsonc` — a parse error → `apply-paranoid-parse-failed`, an unreadable re-read → `apply-paranoid-unreadable`, BOTH roll up to `apply-paranoid-failed` → `failed`/`applied:true` (bytes landed) → recommend rollback; a non-`.json` target is SKIPPED (never read). `parseJsonc` TOLERATES valid JSONC (comments/trailing commas) so a legit settings.json never false-fails (reviewer verified live). New ops-layer-legal imports `readFileSync`+`parseJsonc` (M2-safe — no paths.mjs); never-throws (paranoid read-throw is caught), gate-injected, lock-discipline all preserved; `apply.mjs` 199/200 SLOC (`writeOps` MERGED into `performApply` to stay under the ceiling — behavior-identical deviation, no `mgr-lint-ignore`). **(3) MULTI-OP resume** (`recover-resume.mjs::opsLanded`): DELETED the `ops.length>1` early-refusal — the pre-existing per-op loop now verifies 0..N ops (each target re-hashed vs `sha256(op.content)`; ALL match → `committed`; ANY mismatch/absent/out-of-target/bad-kind → refuse WITHOUT transitioning, recommend `--rollback`; no partial-verification false-commit). **Independent `code-reviewer` (opus) APPROVE 0 Blocker/0 High/0 Medium** — all 8 focus areas verified with file:line (never-throws incl. the paranoid read-throw path, M2-safety static+dynamic, gate-not-bypassed, partial-failure accounting K-1 vs K, commit-incomplete-vs-failed, paranoid no-false-positive on JSONC + `isJsonTarget` case-insensitivity, resume multi-op no-false-commit, falsifiable oracles); 3 LOW (P5 `apply-paranoid-unreadable` test, C5d same-target two-op test, the specific `apply-paranoid-parse-failed` assertion in P2) ALL adopted. LOW-probability (a user rarely snapshots twice in one second) but a real CREATE-path defect — add a collision guard (if the dir exists, bump the id with a suffix, or sub-second precision) or a `snapshot-id-collision` refusal. ## Per-Unit Definition of Done (every work unit, in order)
1. **Regression** — full `node --test` green, no regressions.
2. **Code review** — a SEPARATE `code-reviewer` pass (never self-approve); fix Blocker/High before commit.
3. **Boundary** — edge cases covered (use the `test/fixtures/` corpus: broken / unicode-paths / long-paths / case-insensitive / …).
4. **Acceptance** — falsifiable criterion (golden-file oracle; "matches golden", never "exit 0").
5. **Git** — commit on green; **one file = one commit** (data fixtures may commit per-category); push.

## Environment gotchas (verified on this machine)
- Node **v24.14.0**; runner = `node --test` (zero deps). Run from the repo root.
- The **PowerShell tool is unreliable here** → use the **Bash tool with POSIX paths** (`/c/Dev/Projects/claude-mgr`).
- Windows **Developer Mode is ON** → the dogfood symlink uses `cmd /c mklink /D` (PowerShell `New-Item -SymbolicLink` fails).
- **Subagents may TIME OUT on long tasks here — but do NOT disable/abandon delegation.** The DoD's SEPARATE `code-reviewer` and `executor` passes MUST stay delegated (never self-author + self-approve — that gate is the whole point). Mitigate timeouts by scoping each delegated task SMALL (one sub-unit at a time) and **resuming/retrying** a timed-out agent; fall back to a direct Edit ONLY for a tiny fix a reviewer has already prescribed.
- The tool resolves the governed `~/.claude/` and `~/.claude/hooks/lib` via the home dir — **independent of cwd**, so develop here, not inside `~/.claude/`.
- GitHub remote: `exampleuser-jpg/claude-mgr` (PRIVATE), `main` → `origin/main`.
